Table compliance.enforcement_action {
  enforcement_action_id varchar [pk, note: 'Unique identifier for the enforcement action record. Primary key.']
  compliance_permit_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the permit under which the violation and enforcement action occurred (NPDES permit, drinking water permit, IUP, etc.).']
  facility_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the water treatment plant (WTP), wastewater treatment plant (WWTP), or other facility subject to the enforcement action.']
  regulatory_agency_id varchar [note: 'FK to agency']
  violation_id varchar [note: 'Reference to the primary violation record that triggered this enforcement action. Links to the violation tracking system.']
  water_system_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to quality.water_system. Business justification: System-level enforcement tracking: EPA and state enforcement actions under SDWA are taken against water_systems (by PWSID). This FK enables system-level enforcement history, compliance status assessme']
  wwtp_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to wastewater.wwtp. Business justification: Enforcement actions (NOVs, consent orders, civil penalties) are issued against specific WWTPs for NPDES violations. Direct FK enables enforcement history per WWTP, penalty tracking, and legal response']
  action_date date [note: 'Action date']
  action_number varchar [note: 'Official enforcement action number or case number assigned by the regulatory agency (EPA, state primacy agency, NPDES authority). This is the externally-known identifier used in all regulatory correspondence and legal documents.']
  action_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the enforcement action. Tracks progression from issuance through utility response, negotiation, and final resolution.']
  action_summary varchar [note: 'Brief summary of the enforcement action, including the nature of the violation, regulatory basis, and key requirements. Provides context for reporting and management review.']
  action_type varchar [note: 'Type of formal enforcement action initiated by the regulatory agency. Includes Notice of Violation (NOV), Administrative Order (AO), Consent Order, Compliance Schedule, civil penalty assessment, or criminal referral.']
  appeal_filed_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the utility filed a formal appeal or contested the enforcement action through administrative or judicial proceedings.']
  appeal_filing_date date [note: 'Date the utility filed its appeal or petition for review. Null if no appeal was filed.']
  board_notification_date date [note: 'Date the utility\'s Board of Directors or governing body was notified of the enforcement action. Tracks governance and executive oversight requirements.']
  civil_penalty_amount decimal(15,2) [note: 'Monetary penalty amount assessed by the regulatory agency in U.S. dollars. Null if no civil penalty was imposed.']
  compliance_schedule_final_deadline date [note: 'Final deadline by which all corrective actions and compliance milestones must be completed. Null if no compliance schedule is required.']
  compliance_schedule_required_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the enforcement action includes a formal compliance schedule with milestones and deadlines for corrective actions.']
  corrective_action_required boolean [note: 'Description of the corrective actions required by the enforcement action. May include operational changes, infrastructure upgrades, process improvements, or enhanced monitoring.']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this enforcement action record was first created in the system. Audit trail for data lineage.']
  document_reference_number varchar [note: 'Internal document management system reference number for the enforcement action file. Links to stored correspondence, legal documents, and supporting materials.']
  issue_date date [note: 'Date the enforcement action was officially issued or signed by the regulatory agency. This is the principal business event timestamp for the enforcement action lifecycle.']
  issuing_agency varchar [note: 'Name of the regulatory agency that issued the enforcement action (e.g., U.S. Environmental Protection Agency, State Department of Environmental Quality, Regional Water Quality Control Board).']
  issuing_agency_region varchar [note: 'Regional office, district, or jurisdiction of the issuing agency (e.g., EPA Region 5, Northwest Regional Office). Identifies the specific regulatory authority within the agency structure.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this enforcement action record was last updated. Audit trail for change tracking.']
  legal_counsel_assigned varchar [note: 'Name of the internal or external legal counsel assigned to manage the utility\'s response to the enforcement action. Business-confidential information.']
  legal_firm_name varchar [note: 'Name of the external law firm representing the utility, if external counsel is engaged. Null if handled internally.']
  modified_by_user varchar [note: 'User ID or name of the person who last modified this enforcement action record. Audit trail for accountability.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text notes capturing additional context, internal discussions, negotiation history, or other relevant information not captured in structured fields.']
  penalty_amount decimal(18,2) [note: 'Penalty amount']
  penalty_paid_amount decimal(15,2) [note: 'Actual amount paid by the utility toward the civil penalty. May differ from assessed amount due to negotiated settlements or payment plans.']
  penalty_payment_date date [note: 'Date the civil penalty payment was made to the regulatory agency. Tracks compliance with payment deadlines.']
  public_notice_date date [note: 'Date public notice of the enforcement action was issued. Null if public notice is not required.']
  public_notice_required_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the enforcement action requires public notification under regulatory or consent order terms. Drives public communication and transparency obligations.']
  received_date date [note: 'Date the utility officially received the enforcement action notice. Used to calculate response deadlines and compliance timelines.']
  regulatory_citation varchar [note: 'Specific regulatory statute, rule, or permit condition cited in the enforcement action (e.g., Clean Water Act Section 301, 40 CFR 122.41, NPDES Permit Condition III.A.1). Identifies the legal basis for the enforcement.']
  resolution_date date [note: 'Date the enforcement action was formally resolved or closed. Indicates completion of all required corrective actions, penalty payments, and regulatory obligations.']
  resolution_outcome varchar [note: 'Final outcome of the enforcement action. Indicates how the action was resolved (compliance achieved, consent order executed, penalty paid, dismissed, or under appeal).']
  response_due_date date [note: 'Deadline by which the utility must submit a formal response to the enforcement action. Typically specified in the enforcement notice or calculated based on regulatory timelines.']
  response_submitted_date date [note: 'Date the utility submitted its formal response to the enforcement action. Tracks compliance with response deadlines.']
  sep_description varchar [note: 'Description of the Supplemental Environmental Project (SEP) agreed to as part of the enforcement settlement. Null if no SEP is included.']
  sep_estimated_cost decimal(15,2) [note: 'Estimated cost of the Supplemental Environmental Project (SEP) in U.S. dollars. Used to calculate penalty offsets and track SEP investment.']
  supplemental_environmental_project_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the enforcement action includes a Supplemental Environmental Project (SEP) as part of the settlement. SEPs are environmentally beneficial projects that go beyond compliance requirements and may offset civil penalties.']

  Note: 'Formal enforcement action initiated by a regulatory agency (EPA, state primacy agency, NPDES authority) against the utility in response to violations, including Notices of Violation (NOVs), Administrative Orders (AOs), Consent Orders, Compliance Schedules, civil penalties, and criminal referrals. Tracks the issuing agency, action type, associated violations, compliance schedule milestones, penalty amounts, response deadlines, legal counsel assigned, and resolution outcome. Drives the utility\'s formal regulatory response process.'
}

  regulatory_requirement_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to compliance.regulatory_requirement.   water_system_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to quality.water_system. This FK enables tracking all submissions per water system']
  wwtp_id varchar [note: 'Foreign key linking to wastewater.wwtp. Business justification: WWTPs submit Discharge Monitoring Reports (DMRs) and other NPDES regulatory submissions. Direct FK enables DMR submission history per WWTP, late submission tracking, and agency acknowledgment manageme']

  acknowledgment_reference_number varchar [note: 'The confirmation or tracking number provided by the regulatory agency upon receipt of the submission.']
  agency_comments varchar [note: 'Comments, feedback, or instructions provided by the regulatory agency regarding the submission.']
  agency_response_date date [note: 'The date on which the regulatory agency provided a formal response, feedback, or determination regarding the submission.']
  agency_response_type varchar [note: 'The type of response or action taken by the regulatory agency in response to the submission.']

  exceedance_count varchar [note: 'The number of parameter exceedances (values above permit limits but not necessarily violations) reported in this submission.']

  is_late_submission boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the submission was filed after the regulatory due date, which may trigger enforcement action or violation notices.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'The timestamp when this regulatory submission record was last updated or modified.']

  public_notice_date date [note: 'The date on which public notification was issued, if required.']
  public_notice_required boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this submission requires public notification (e.g., CCR publication, SSO public notice, boil water advisory).']
  reporting_period_end_date date [note: 'The ending date of the time period covered by this regulatory submission.']
  reporting_period_start_date date [note: 'The beginning date of the time period covered by this regulatory submission.']
  resubmission_required boolean [note: 'Indicates whether the regulatory agency has requested a corrected or amended resubmission of the report.']

  submission_method varchar [note: 'The method or channel used to submit the report to the regulatory agency. NetDMR is the EPA electronic discharge monitoring reporting system.']
  submission_notes varchar [note: 'Internal notes, comments, or additional context regarding the preparation, submission, or follow-up actions for this regulatory submission.']
  submission_number varchar [note: 'Business identifier or tracking number assigned to the regulatory submission, often used for external reference and correspondence with regulatory agencies.']
  submission_status varchar [note: 'Current lifecycle status of the regulatory submission indicating its progress through the submission and review workflow.']
  submission_type varchar [note: 'Category of regulatory submission. DMR = Discharge Monitoring Report, MOR = Monthly Operating Report, CCR = Consumer Confidence Report, SSO = Sanitary Sewer Overflow, CSO = Combined Sewer Overflow, PFAS = Per- and Polyfluoroalkyl Substances, LCRR = Lead and Copper Rule Revisions. [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: DMR|MOR|CCR|SSO_notification|CSO_notification|pretreatment_report|annual_report|PFAS_report|LCRR_inventory|permit_application|variance_request|other — promote to reference product]']
  violation_count varchar [note: 'The number of permit limit violations or non-compliance events reported in this submission.']

  Note: 'Master record of all formal regulatory submissions made by the utility to regulatory agencies, serving as the single audit trail for submission compliance. Covers DMR submissions (via NetDMR), MOR submissions, CCR certifications, annual compliance reports, pretreatment program reports, SSO/CSO notifications, PFAS reporting, LCRR service line inventory submissions, and Lead Service Line Replacement (LSLR) progress reports. Tracks submission type, receiving agency, submission date, submission method (NetDMR, state portal, paper, email), reporting period, submitter, certifying official, certification status, acknowledgment receipt, late submission flags, and resubmission history. Enables monitoring of submission timeliness — a key compliance metric tracked by state primacy agencies.'
}

  agency_code varchar [note: 'Short alphanumeric code uniquely identifying the regulatory agency within the utility\'s systems (e.g., EPA_R5, STATE_DNR, PUC_WI).']

  agency_main_phone varchar [note: 'Main switchboard or general inquiry phone number for the regulatory agency.']

  agency_short_name varchar [note: 'Abbreviated or commonly used name for the agency (e.g., EPA Region 5, WI DNR, OSHA).']
  agency_status varchar [note: 'Current operational status of the regulatory agency (active, inactive, merged, dissolved).']
  agency_type varchar [note: 'Classification of the regulatory agency by its primary regulatory focus (environmental, health, safety, rate regulatory, labor, quality standards, other). [ENUM-REF-CANDIDATE: environmental|health|safety|rate_regulatory|labor|quality_standards|other — 7 candidates stripped; promote to reference product]']
  agency_website_url varchar [note: 'Official website URL for the regulatory agency.']
  business_hours varchar [note: 'Standard business hours of operation for the regulatory agency office (e.g., Monday-Friday 8:00 AM - 5:00 PM PST).']
  city varchar [note: 'City name for the agency\'s physical mailing address.']
  contact_email varchar
  contact_name varchar [note: 'Contact name']
  contact_phone varchar
  country_code varchar [note: 'Three-letter ISO country code for the agency\'s physical mailing address (e.g., USA, CAN, MEX).']
  created_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this regulatory agency record was first created in the system.']

  enforcement_authority_level varchar [note: 'Level of enforcement authority this agency holds over the utility (primary, delegated, advisory, none).   eu_directive_scope varchar [note: 'Comma-separated list of EU directives this agency administers (DWD_2020_2184, REACH, WFD_2000_60, UWWTD_91_271).']
  eu_member_state varchar [note: 'For EU-region agencies, the EU member state code (e.g. DE, FR, NL). NULL for non-EU agencies.']
  eu_member_state_code varchar [note: 'ISO 3166-1 alpha-2 code for EU member state where this agency has competent authority (e.g. DE, FR, NL). NULL for non-EU agencies.']
  eu_reference_path varchar [note: 'EU reference path: Drinking Water Directive 2020/2184; REACH; WFD; UWWTD citation chain.']
  eu_regulatory_framework varchar [note: 'EU directives administered (e.g. Drinking Water Directive 2020/2184,REACH,Water Framework Directive,Urban Wastewater Treatment Directive). REACH restriction targets broader PFAS class, not individual compounds; WFD defines surface-water status differently']
  fax_number varchar [note: 'Fax number for document submission to the regulatory agency, if applicable.']
  inspection_frequency_months varchar [note: 'Typical frequency in months at which this regulatory agency conducts inspections of utility facilities under its jurisdiction.']
  inspection_frequency_typical varchar [note: 'Typical frequency at which this agency conducts inspections or audits of utility facilities (annual, biennial, triennial, as-needed, risk-based).']
  international_agency_flag boolean [note: 'True for non-US (EU/FR/UK/DE) regulatory agencies.']
  is_active boolean
  jurisdiction varchar [note: 'Geographic or administrative jurisdiction of the regulatory agency (e.g., United States, California, Los Angeles County).']
  jurisdiction_code varchar [note: 'Jurisdiction code']
  jurisdiction_geographic_area varchar [note: 'Geographic area or service territory over which the agency has regulatory authority (e.g., EPA Region 5 covers IL, IN, MI, MN, OH, WI; or specific county/municipality names).']
  jurisdiction_level varchar [note: 'The governmental level at which the agency operates (federal, state, regional, local, international).']
  last_inspection_date date [note: 'Date of the most recent inspection conducted by this regulatory agency at any utility facility.']
  last_modified_timestamp timestamp [note: 'Timestamp when this regulatory agency record was last updated or modified.']
  notes varchar [note: 'Free-text field for additional notes, special instructions, or context about the regulatory agency relationship.']
  notification_deadline_hours varchar [note: 'Standard number of hours within which the utility must notify this agency of reportable incidents or violations (e.g., 24 hours for SSO events).']
  npdes_authority_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this agency has authority to issue and enforce NPDES permits under the Clean Water Act. True if authorized, False otherwise.']
  parent_regulatory_agency_id_legacy varchar [note: 'Reference to the parent or umbrella agency if this agency is a regional office, division, or sub-agency (e.g., EPA Region 5 parent is EPA). Null if this is a top-level agency.']
  postal_code varchar [note: 'Postal or ZIP code for the agency\'s physical mailing address.']
  pretreatment_authority_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this agency has authority to oversee industrial pretreatment programs. True if authorized, False otherwise.']
  primacy_agency_flag boolean [note: 'Indicates whether this agency has primacy authority for Safe Drinking Water Act (SDWA) enforcement in its jurisdiction. True if primacy agency, False otherwise.']
  primacy_status varchar [note: 'Indicates whether this agency is a primacy agency under the Safe Drinking Water Act (SDWA) or Clean Water Act (CWA), meaning it has been delegated primary enforcement authority by EPA (primacy_agency, non_primacy, not_applicable).']
  primary_contact_email varchar [note: 'Primary email address for the agency contact.']
  primary_contact_name varchar [note: 'Full name of the primary contact person at the agency for utility compliance matters.']
  primary_contact_phone varchar [note: 'Primary telephone number for the agency contact.']
  primary_contact_title varchar [note: 'Job title or role of the primary contact person at the agency.']
  primary_program varchar
  primary_regulatory_program varchar [note: 'The main regulatory program or statute administered by this agency relevant to water utilities (e.g., SDWA, CWA, NPDES, OSHA, Rate Regulation).']
  region_code varchar [note: 'Regional designation or code if the agency operates within a specific region (e.g., EPA Region 9, Water Board Region 4).']
  regulatory_framework varchar [note: 'Applicable regulatory framework for the region (US=EPA/AWWA/NPDWR/UCMR/NPDES; EU=Drinking Water Directive 2020/2184; REACH; Water Framework Directive; Urban Wastewater Treatment Directive; OTHER=Other national/regional frameworks).']
  regulatory_program varchar [note: 'Primary regulatory program or framework administered by the agency (e.g., NPDES, SDWA Primacy, Pretreatment, Lead and Copper Rule).']
  regulatory_region varchar [note: 'Regulatory region Allowed regions: US,EU,OTHER.']
  regulatory_region_code varchar [note: 'ISO region code identifying the jurisdiction this agency operates in (US, EU, OTHER). Enables multi-jurisdictional regulatory agency modeling.']
  reporting_frequency_default varchar [note: 'Default or most common reporting frequency required by this agency for compliance reports (monthly, quarterly, semi-annual, annual, event-driven, as-required).']
  reporting_system_name varchar [note: 'Name of the electronic reporting system used by the agency (e.g., NetDMR, SDWIS, state-specific portal).']
  state varchar [note: 'Two-letter state or province code where the regulatory agency office is located.']
  state_province varchar [note: 'Two-letter state or province code for the agency\'s physical mailing address (e.g., WI, IL, CA).']
  submission_credentials_reference varchar [note: 'Reference identifier or location for stored login credentials or API keys used to access the agency\'s submission portal. Should reference a secure credential vault, not store actual credentials.']
  submission_portal_name varchar [note: 'Name of the online submission portal or system (e.g., NetDMR, State Environmental Portal, OSHA Injury Tracking Application).']
  submission_portal_url varchar [note: 'URL for the online portal or system used to submit compliance reports, permits, or other regulatory documents to this agency (e.g., NetDMR, state e-reporting system).']
  termination_date date [note: 'Date when this agency\'s jurisdiction or regulatory authority over the utility ended or will end. Null if still active.']
  us_reference_path varchar [note: 'US reference path: EPA/AWWA/NPDWR/UCMR/NPDES citation chain.']
  us_regulatory_framework varchar [note: 'US frameworks administered (e.g. EPA,AWWA,NPDWR,UCMR,NPDES).']
  website_url varchar [note: 'Official website URL for the regulatory agency.']

  Note: 'Master reference table for regulatory_agency. Referenced by: compliance.regulatory_submission.regulatory_agency_id, treatment.mor_submission.regulatory_agency_id, treatment.treatment_permit.regulatory_agency_id, treatment.treatment_violation.regulatory_agency_id'
}
